-- Dumps a natives table from game's memory
local baseAddr=0x142B5ED10	-- Current base addr for 1.0.757.4
--
function int2hex(int, size)	-- Print hex formatted integer as <size> bytes
	size = size or 1
	size = size * 2
	return string.upper(string.format("%0"..size.."x", int))
end
--
print("-----------------------------------------------------------------")
--
for i=0,255 do	-- Scans for natives ending 00-FF
	local basePointer = baseAddr+(i*8)    -- Pointer to the first block in memory
	print("Natives ending in 0x"..int2hex(i),"base pointer is","0x"..int2hex(readInteger(basePointer), 4))
	local blockAddr = readInteger(basePointer)	-- Address of the first block
	local active = true
	while active do
		local nextBlock = readInteger(blockAddr)	-- Next block = offset 0
		local nativesBase = blockAddr+64			-- Natives table inside the block
		local nNatives = readInteger(nativesBase)	-- Number of natives in this block
		print("  Block: 0x"..int2hex(blockAddr, 4),"has",nNatives,"natives. Next block -> 0x"..int2hex(nextBlock, 4))
		for j=1,nNatives do							-- Print all the natives in this block and its pointers
			local nativeAddr = nativesBase+(j*8)
			local pointerAddr = blockAddr+(j*8)
			local n1 = int2hex(readInteger(nativeAddr), 4)
			local n2 = int2hex(readInteger(nativeAddr+4), 4)
			local pointer = int2hex(readInteger(pointerAddr), 4)
			print("       0x"..n2..n1.." : 0x1"..pointer)
		end
		if nextBlock == 0 then
			active = false
		else
			blockAddr = nextBlock
		end
	end
end
